    var getCookieVal = function(cookieName, key) {
        var cookies = "",
            result = "",
            match = false;

        match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp(cookieName + "=([^;]+)"));

        if (match) {
            cookies = match[1];
        }

        cookies.split("&").forEach(function (item) {
            var temp = item.split("=");
            if (temp[0] === key) {
                result = temp[1];
            }
        });
        return result;
    }

   document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
            var cssFiles = [];

                cssFiles.push("https://s3.images-iherb.com/static/catalog/desktop/iherb/header-footer.min_ef210ec4c77ebf37957ef5b9c6093490.css");

            var head = document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0];

                link.href = file;
                head.appendChild(link);
            });

  <script type="text/javascript">
   document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
        var jsFiles = [];


                jsFiles.push("https://s3.images-iherb.com/static/catalog/desktop/iherb/home.min_16058d9059956c5a3c40fcf834675ae7.js");

        function loadJS(file) {
            var script = document.createElement("script");
            script.type = "text/javascript";
            script.src = file;
            document.body.appendChild(script);
        }

        function addBodyScripts() {
            for (var i = 0; i < jsFiles.length; i++) {
                loadJS(jsFiles[i]);
            }
        }

        var head = document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0];
        var script = document.createElement('script');
        if (typeof jQuery == 'undefined') {
            script.type = 'text/javascript';
            script.src = 'https://s3.images-iherb.com/static/js/vendor/jquery-1.12.4.min.js';
            script.onload = addBodyScripts;
            head.appendChild(script);
        }
        else {
            addBodyScripts();
        }

        var loaderCheckFinished = setInterval(function () {
            var deferBlock = document.getElementsByClassName("defer-block");
            if (deferBlock.length > 0 && window.getComputedStyle(deferBlock[0])["display"] === "block") {
                // Stops the load spinner once the panel-stack CSS (in grid) is loaded.
                var loadSpinner = document.getElementsByClassName("loader");
                if (loadSpinner.length > 0) {
                    loadSpinner[0].className = "loader";
                    clearInterval(loaderCheckFinished);
                }
            }
        }, 100);
        var loaderCheckFinished2 = setInterval(function () {
            var panelStackBlock = document.getElementsByClassName("panel-stack");
            if (panelStackBlock.length > 0 && window.getComputedStyle(panelStackBlock[0])["display"] === "block") {
                // Stops the load spinner once the panel-stack CSS (in grid) is loaded.
                var loadSpinner = document.getElementsByClassName("loader");
                if (loadSpinner.length > 0) {
                    loadSpinner[0].className = "loader";
                }
                clearInterval(loaderCheckFinished2);
            }
        }, 100);
    });
  </script>

   window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
        window.dataLayer.push({
            'countryCode': location.hostname.indexOf(".iherb.") >= 0 ? location.hostname.split(".")[0].toUpperCase() : "TEST",
            'currentDevice': '1'

  <script>
   (function () {
                function getCookieVal (cookieName, key) {
                    var cookies = '',
                        result = '',
                        match = false;

                    match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp(cookieName + '=([^;]+)'));
                    if (match) {
                        cookies = match[1];
                    }

                    cookies.split('&').forEach(function (item) {
                        var temp = item.split('=');
                        if (temp[0] === key) {
                            result = temp[1];
                        }
                    });
                    return result;
                }

                var customerId = getCookieVal("ihr-temse", "tempses");

                window.dataLayer.push({
                    uid: customerId
                });

                if (window.ih) {
                    ih.ga.prod.setCurrency('USD');
                }
            })();
  </script>
  <!-- Userway Widget -->
  <script type="text/javascript">
   var _userway_config = {
                account: "8UEIqHykLW"
            };
            window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(event) {
                var userwayReady = false;
                var userwayNullCheck = document.getElementsByClassName("userway-widget").length > 0;
                if(userwayNullCheck) {
                    document.getElementsByClassName("userway-widget")[0].addEventListener("click",function(e){
                        e.preventDefault();
                        if(document.getElementById("userway-widget-js") == null) {
                            var uw = document.createElement("script");
                            uw.src = "https://cdn.userway.org/widget.js";
                            uw.id = "userway-widget-js";
                            var s = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
                            s.parentNode.insertBefore(uw, s);
                            document.addEventListener("userway:init_completed", function(e) {
                                var uw_instance = e.detail.userWayInstance;
                                if (uw_instance) {
                                    userwayReady = true;
                                    UserWay.widgetOpen();
                                } else {
                                    console.error('No UserWay instance found in payload');
                                }
                            });
                        }
                        if (userwayReady) {
                            UserWay.widgetOpen();
                        }
                    });
                }
            });
  </script>
